## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Start
    Start --> PrepareButtons : initialize buttonConfig
    PrepareButtons --> SetTitleDefault : title = BackgroundPackageErrorTitle
    SetTitleDefault --> CheckNetwork
    CheckNetwork --> NetworkCase : e instanceof NetworkError
    CheckNetwork --> DebugCase : else
    NetworkCase --> BuildNetworkDescription
    BuildNetworkDescription --> CallAlert
    DebugCase --> BuildDebugDescription
    BuildDebugDescription --> CallAlert
    CallAlert --> [*]
```
